<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-442"><dt><span id="_transmit_as__must_specify_a_transmissible_type"></span><span id="_TRANSMIT_AS__MUST_SPECIFY_A_TRANSMISSIBLE_TYPE"></span>[transmit_as] è necessario specificare un tipo trasmissibile</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-442"><dt><span id="_transmit_as__must_specify_a_transmissible_type"></span><span id="_TRANSMIT_AS__MUST_SPECIFY_A_TRANSMISSIBLE_TYPE"></span>[transmit_as] must specify a transmissible type</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-443">Il tipo [<a href="transmit-as.md"><strong>transmit_as</strong></a>] specificato deriva da un tipo che non può essere trasmesso da Microsoft RPC, ad esempio <a href="void.md"><strong>void</strong></a>, <strong>void \*</strong>o <a href="int.md"><strong>int</strong></a>. Utilizzare un tipo di base RPC definito; nel caso di <strong>int</strong>, aggiungere identificatori di dimensioni come <a href="small.md"><strong>small</strong></a>, <a href="short.md"><strong>short</strong></a>o <a href="long.md"><strong>Long</strong></a> per qualificare <strong>int</strong>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-443">The specified [<a href="transmit-as.md"><strong>transmit_as</strong></a>] type derives from a type that cannot be transmitted by Microsoft RPC, such as <a href="void.md"><strong>void</strong></a>, <strong>void \*</strong>, or <a href="int.md"><strong>int</strong></a>. Use a defined RPC base type; in the case of <strong>int</strong>, add size specifiers like <a href="small.md"><strong>small</strong></a>, <a href="short.md"><strong>short</strong></a>, or <a href="long.md"><strong>long</strong></a> to qualify the <strong>int</strong>.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

ICF &quot; )] o optimize [( &quot; s &quot; )] alla funzione nel file ACF.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1481">The optimization mode may be changed on the command line by specifying -Oicf or -Os instead of -Oi or by adding an [optimize9&quot;icf&quot;)] or optimize[(&quot;s&quot;)] attribute to the function in the ACF file.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1482">Questo avviso si verifica in genere quando si passano strutture di grandi dimensioni come parametri per valore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1482">This warning typically happens when passing large structures as parameters by value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1483">La dimensione dello stack necessaria può essere ridotta passando un puntatore alla struttura.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1483">The required stack size can be lowered by passing a pointer to the structure instead.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1484">Esempio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1484">Example:</span></span><br/>

// workaround: pass by reference

data-stu-id="568c2-1657">This message may be accompanied by a diagnostic printout with additional information about the problem.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1658">Se viene visualizzato questo errore, segnalare un bug a Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1658">If yoiu see this error, report a bug to Microsoft.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1659">Specificare i file IDL, i file ACF, la riga di comando MIDL completa e l'output di diagnostica, se presenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1659">Specify your IDL files, ACF files, full MIDL command line, and diagnostic output, if any.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1661"><dt><span id="SAFEARRAY_roo__syntax_is_not_supported_outside_of_the_library_block__use_LPSAFEARRAY_for_proxy"></span><span id="safearray_roo__syntax_is_not_supported_outside_of_the_library_block__use_lpsafearray_for_proxy"></span><span id="SAFEARRAY_ROO__SYNTAX_IS_NOT_SUPPORTED_OUTSIDE_OF_THE_LIBRARY_BLOCK__USE_LPSAFEARRAY_FOR_PROXY"></span>La sintassi SAFEARRAY (Roo) non è supportata all'esterno del blocco di libreria. usare LPSAFEARRAY per il proxy</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1661"><dt><span id="SAFEARRAY_roo__syntax_is_not_supported_outside_of_the_library_block__use_LPSAFEARRAY_for_proxy"></span><span id="safearray_roo__syntax_is_not_supported_outside_of_the_library_block__use_lpsafearray_for_proxy"></span><span id="SAFEARRAY_ROO__SYNTAX_IS_NOT_SUPPORTED_OUTSIDE_OF_THE_LIBRARY_BLOCK__USE_LPSAFEARRAY_FOR_PROXY"></span>SAFEARRAY(roo) syntax is not supported outside of the library block, use LPSAFEARRAY for proxy</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1662">I SAFEARRAY tipizzati in modo esplicito non sono consentiti all'esterno di un blocco di libreria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1662">Explicitly-typed SAFEARRAYs are not allowed outside of a library block.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1663">In alternativa, usare LPSAFEARRAY.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1663">Use LPSAFEARRAY instead.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1664">Nell'esempio seguente viene illustrato questo errore:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1664">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>void roo(SAFEARRAY(long) *a); //MIDL2412 when outside a library block
void roo(LPSAFEAEEAY a);         //OK</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>

<td><span id="MIDL2414"></span><span id="midl2414"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1669"><dt><strong>MIDL2414</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1669"><dt><strong>MIDL2414</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1670"><dt><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-Oicf__using_-OI"></span><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-oicf__using_-oi"></span><span id="FLOATING_POINT_OR_COMPLEX_RETURN_TYPES_WITH__DECODE__ARE_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_-OICF__USING_-OI"></span>i tipi restituiti a virgola mobile o complessi con [Decode] non sono supportati in-Oicf, using-OI</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1670"><dt><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-Oicf__using_-OI"></span><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-oicf__using_-oi"></span><span id="FLOATING_POINT_OR_COMPLEX_RETURN_TYPES_WITH__DECODE__ARE_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_-OICF__USING_-OI"></span>floating point or complex return types with [decode] are not supported in -Oicf, using -OI</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1671">Le procedure con tipi restituiti a virgola mobile o di struttura/Unione non sono supportate nella selezione dello stile-Oicf.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1671">Procedures with floating point or structure/union return types are not supported in the -Oicf style pickling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1672">Una soluzione alternativa per 32 bit prevede l'uso della modalità di ottimizzazione-OI durante la serializzazione dei dati (tramite [Encode] e/o [Decode]).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1672">A work around for 32-bit is to use the -Oi optimization mode when serializing data (using [encode] and/or [decode]).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1673">Tuttavia, dato che l'interprete di stile obsoleto e il supporto per la selezione vengono suddivisi in più fasi dopo la versione di Windows 2000, l'utilizzo di puntatori è fortemente suggerito come soluzione per questo problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1673">However, as the old -Oi style interpreter and pickling support are slated to be phased out after the Windows 2000 release, using pointers is strongly suggested as the work around for this problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1674">Si noti anche che, in genere, la modifica di un metodo di interfaccia per l'uso di un puntatore [out, Ref] anziché del valore restituito che causa il problema è completamente compatibile con le versioni precedenti in transito e può essere facilmente nascosta a livello di app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1674">Also note that typically, changing an interface method to use an [out, ref] pointer instead of the return value causing the problem is fully backward-compatible on wire and can be easily hidden from the app layer.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1675">Questo avviso può essere eliminato globalmente specificando-OI sulla riga di comando MIDL o per una singola funzione aggiungendo l'attributo [Optimize ( &quot; i &quot; )] alla funzione nel file ACF.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1675">This warning can be suppressed globally by specifying -Oi on the MIDL command line or for an individual function by adding the [optimize(&quot;i&quot;)] attribute to the function in the ACF file.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1676">Nell'esempio seguente viene illustrato il problema:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1676">The following example demonstrates the issue:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1677">Roo. idl:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1677">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>double GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="568c2-1678">Roo. ACF:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1678">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="568c2-1679">Una delle opzioni per ovviare a questa limitazione consiste nel passare un parametro [out] per contenere il risultato invece di usare un valore restituito:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1679">One option to work around this limitation would be to pass an [out] parameter to hold the result instead of using a return value:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1680">Roo. idl:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1680">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>void GetDouble([out] double *result); //top level pointer is a [ref] pointer</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="568c2-1681">Roo. ACF:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1681">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="568c2-1682">Come indicato in precedenza, la soluzione descritta in precedenza è efficace non solo per le nuove interfacce, ma anche per risolvere i vecchi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1682">As mentioned earlier, the solution described above is good not only for the new interfaces but also as a work-around for the old ones.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1683">La rappresentazione in transito per il &quot; nuovo &quot; argomento out è uguale a quella del valore restituito (si noti void come nuovo valore restituito).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1683">The wire representation for the new &quot;out&quot; argument is the same as for the return value (notice void as the new return value).</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

return type is not supported for 64-bit when using [decode]</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1686">Le procedure con tipi restituiti a virgola mobile o di struttura/Unione non sono data-ttu-id="568c2-1689">Nell'esempio seguente viene illustrato questo errore:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1689">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1690">Roo. idl:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1690">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>double GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="568c2-1691">Roo. ACF:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1691">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="568c2-1692">Di seguito sono riportate le opzioni consigliate per le interfacce nuove e precedenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1692">The following is advised as a work-around for both new and old interfaces.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1693">Usare un parametro [out] per conservare il risultato invece di usare un valore restituito:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1693">Use an [out] parameter to hold the result instead of using a return value:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1694">Roo. idl:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1694">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="568c2-1695">Roo. ACF:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1695">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="568c2-1696">Si noti che questa soluzione è completamente compatibile con le versioni precedenti in transito, in quanto la rappresentazione in transito di un puntatore [Ref, out] o un valore Double corrisponde a quella di un valore Double.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1696">Note that this solution is fully backward-compatible on wire, as the wire representation of a [ref, out] pointer or a double is the same as that of a double.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

st2:

<td><span id="MIDL2465"></span><span id="midl2465"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1714"><dt><strong>MIDL2465</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1714"><dt><strong>MIDL2465</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1715"><dt><span id="Structures_containing_conformant_arrays_must_be_passed_by_reference"></span><span id="structures_containing_conformant_arrays_must_be_passed_by_reference"></span><span id="STRUCTURES_CONTAINING_CONFORMANT_ARRAYS_MUST_BE_PASSED_BY_REFERENCE"></span>Le strutture contenenti matrici conformi devono essere passate per riferimento</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1715"><dt><span id="Structures_containing_conformant_arrays_must_be_passed_by_reference"></span><span id="structures_containing_conformant_arrays_must_be_passed_by_reference"></span><span id="STRUCTURES_CONTAINING_CONFORMANT_ARRAYS_MUST_BE_PASSED_BY_REFERENCE"></span>Structures containing conformant arrays must be passed by reference</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1716">I parametri di primo livello in RPC devono avere una dimensione ben definita in fase di compilazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1716">Top level parameters in RPC must have a well-defined size at compile time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1717">Non possono essere, né contenere matrici conformi o di dimensioni variabili.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1717">They cannot be, nor contain conformant or varying-sized array.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1718">Inoltre, gli utenti non possono codificare/decodificare un tipo senza dimensioni ben definite.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1718">In addition, users cannot encode/decode a type without well-defined size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1719">Per riferimento, le applicazioni devono passare lo struct o la struttura variabile conforme in base al riferimento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1719">Applications need to pass conformant struct/conformant varying struct by reference.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1720">Nell'esempio seguente viene illustrato questo errore:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1720">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>typedef struct        //Type contains variable-sized array
{
    long s;
    [size_is(s)] char a[];
}
st1;
void roo(st1 s);        //MIDL2465
 
on .acf file
typedef [encode,decode] st1; //MIDL2465</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>
</tr>
<tr class="odd">
<td><span id="MIDL9008"></span><span id="midl9008"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1721"><dt><strong>MIDL9008</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1721"><dt><strong>MIDL9008</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1722"><dt><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._See_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._see_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_INTERNAL_COMPILER_PROBLEM__SYSTEM_ERROR_CODE__-_THE_COMPILER_CANNOT_CONTINUE_FOR_AN_UNKNOWN_REASON._SEE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_A_WORKAROUND."></span> problema interno <system error code> - del compilatore il compilatore non può continuare per un motivo sconosciuto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1722"><dt><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._See_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._see_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_INTERNAL_COMPILER_PROBLEM__SYSTEM_ERROR_CODE__-_THE_COMPILER_CANNOT_CONTINUE_FOR_AN_UNKNOWN_REASON._SEE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_A_WORKAROUND."></span> internal compiler problem <system error code> - the compiler cannot continue for an unknown reason.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1723">Per una soluzione alternativa, vedere la documentazione.</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1723">See documentation for a workaround.</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1724">Il compilatore non è stato in grado di continuare e la relativa origine è sconosciuta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1724">The compiler could not continue and the cause of the error is unknown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1725">Il numero di errore esadecimale è un identificatore di errore di sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1725">The hexadecimal error number is a system-error identifier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1726">La compilazione potrebbe non essere riuscita a causa di un problema esterno, ad esempio una condizione di memoria insufficiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1726">The compile may have failed because of an external problem, such as an out-of-memory condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1727">In tal caso, è possibile trovare altre informazioni in Winerror. h o NTSTATUS. h.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1727">In that case, you can find more information in Winerror.h or Ntstatus.h.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1728">Esistono due situazioni che in genere generano questo errore:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1728">There are two situations that usually generate this error:</span></span><br/>
<ul>
<li><span data-ttu-id="568c2-1729">Non è stato possibile ripristinare il compilatore MIDL dopo aver rilevato un errore nel file IDL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1729">The MIDL compiler failed to recover after detecting an error in the IDL file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1730">Se MIDL ha restituito tutti i messaggi di errore relativi al file IDL, provare a correggerli e a ricompilarli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1730">If MIDL returned any error messages about your IDL file, try fixing them and recompiling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1731">Se non sono presenti messaggi di errore, il compilatore potrebbe avere avuto esito negativo prima di segnalare un errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1731">If there are no error messages, the compiler may have failed before it could report an error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1732">Cercare un errore di sintassi sulla riga per cui viene segnalato l'errore interno del compilatore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1732">Look for a syntax error on the line for which the internal compiler error is reported.</span></span></li>
<li><span data-ttu-id="568c2-1733">Il compilatore MIDL non è riuscito a generare il codice corretto con un'opzione di ottimizzazione specificata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1733">The MIDL compiler could not generate correct code under a specified optimization option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1734">Provare a modificare le modalità del compilatore, a compilare l'ottimizzazione in modalità mista (/<a href="-os.md"><strong>OS</strong></a>) o a rimuovere tutte le ottimizzazioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1734">Try changing compiler modes, compiling in mixed-mode optimization (/<a href="-os.md"><strong>Os</strong></a>), or removing all optimizations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1735">In alternativa, ricompilare usando il flag/NO_FORMAT_OPT per disattivare l'ottimizzazione predefinita di MIDL dei descrittori di routine e di tipo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1735">Or, recompile using the /NO_FORMAT_OPT flag to suppress MIDL's default optimization of procedure and type descriptors.</span></span></li>
</ul>
<span data-ttu-id="568c2-1736">Occasionalmente questo errore si verifica anche quando il file IDL è corretto e non vengono utilizzate opzioni di ottimizzazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1736">Occasionally this error occurs even when the IDL file is correct and no optimization options are being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1737">In tal caso, provare a riscrivere la sezione del codice nella posizione in cui è stato segnalato l'errore rimuovendo eventuali modifiche recenti, semplificando o ridisponendo i tipi di dati, modificando i prototipi oppure iniziando a impostare come commento parti del file IDL per individuare il codice del problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1737">If this is the case, try rewriting the section of code in the vicinity of where the error was reported by removing any recent modifications, simplifying or rearranging data types, changing prototypes, or else begin to comment out portions of the IDL file to locate the problem code.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="568c2-1738">Se nessuna di queste opzioni funziona o se si ritiene che il problema sia correlato a un bug in Midl.exe, inviare una notifica a Microsoft, fornendo tutti i dettagli pertinenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="568c2-1738">If none of these options works, or if you think the problem may be related to a bug in Midl.exe, please notify Microsoft, giving all the relevant details.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>
